GALLANTRY AWARDS
IT is hereby notified that HIS EXCELLENCY the PRESIDENT of the Democratic Socialist Republic of Sri Lanka and Commander-in-
Chief of the Armed Forces has been graciously pleased to confer the Gallantry Award of Weerodhara Vibhushanaya, Weera
Wickerama Vibhushanaya, Rana Wicrema Padakkama, Rana Sura Padakkama on the 15th day of July in the year Two Thousand
Thirteen, to the persons named in the Schedule hereto.
By His Excellency's Command.
G
OTABAYA RAJAPAKSA RWP RSP psc
Secretary,
Ministry of Defence and Urban Development.
At the Colombo,
15 July, 2013.

N. B.—This Gazette is printed in Sinhala, Tamil and English Separately.
